Backend Developer)\n\n| Route Path               | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File             | Context Variables                                                                                                    |\n|--------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| /                        | root_redirect           | GET            | -                         | - Redirects to `/dashboard`                                                                                         |\n| /dashboard               | dashboard_page          | GET            | dashboard.html            | featured_songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, album_name: str, duration: int}\ntrending_artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} |\n| /songs                   | song_catalog_page       | GET            | song_catalog.html         | songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, album_name: str, genre: str, duration: int}\ngenres: list of str (genre names for dropdown) |\n| /songs/search            | song_catalog_search     | POST           | song_catalog.html         | songs: filtered list (same structure as `/songs` GET)\ngenres: list of str | \n| /songs/<int:song_id>     | song_details_page       | GET            | song_details.html         | song: dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_id: int, artist_name: str, album_id: int, album_name: str, duration: int, genre: str, release_date: str}\n |\n| /playlists               | playlists_page          | GET            | playlists.html            | playlists: list of dict {playlist_id: int, title: str, description: str, creation_date: str, total_songs: int}         |\n| /playlists/create        | create_playlist_page    | GET            | create_playlist.html      | -                                                                                                                   |\n| /playlists/create        | create_playlist_submit  | POST           | - (redirect after creation)| Form fields: title (str), description (str)                                                                           |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id> | playlist_details_page  | GET            | playlist_details.html      | playlist: dict {playlist_id: int, title: str, description: str, creation_date: str, total_songs: int}\nsongs_in_playlist: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id>/delete | delete_playlist | POST           | - (redirect after deletion) | playlist_id: int                                                                                                |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id>/remove_song/<int:song_id> | remove_song_from_playlist | POST | - (redirect after removal) | playlist_id: int, song_id: int                                                                                       |\n| /albums                  | albums_page             | GET            | albums.html               | albums: list of dict {album_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, release_year: int, genre: str}                     |\n| /albums/search           | albums_search           | POST           | albums.html               | albums: filtered list (same structure as `/albums` GET)                                                             |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>   | album_details_page      | GET            | album_details.html        | album: dict {album_id: int, title: str, artist_id: int, artist_name: str, release_year: int, total_songs: int, genre: str}\nsongs_in_album: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, duration: int} |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>/add_all_to_playlist | add_album_to_playlist | POST | - (redirect after action) | album_id: int, playlist_id: int                                                                                      |\n| /artists                 | artists_page            | GET            | artists.html              | artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str, country: str, formation_year: int}                       |\n| /artists/search          | artists_search          | POST           | artists.html              | artists: filtered list (same structure as `/artists` GET)                                                           |\n| /artists/<int:artist_id> | artist_profile_page     | GET            | artist_profile.html       | artist: dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str, country: str, formation_year: int}\nsongs_by_artist: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, album_name: str, duration: int} |\n| /genres                  | genre_exploration_page  | GET            | genres.html               | genres: list of dict {genre_id: int, genre_name: str, description: str}\nselected_genre_songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} (optional)\nselected_genre_artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} (optional)\nselected_genre: str (genre name, optional) |\n| /genres/select           | genre_select            | POST           | genres.html               | Same as GET `/genres` plus selected_genre: str                                                                        |\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)\n\n---\n\n### Template: dashboard.html\n- Template File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div)\n  - `featured-songs` (Div)\n  - `browse-songs-button` (Button)\n  - `my-playlists-button` (Button)\n  - `trending-artists-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `featured_songs`: List of dicts with keys: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `album_name`(str), `duration`(int seconds)\n  - `trending_artists`: List of dicts with keys: `artist_id`(int), `name`(str), `genre`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `browse-songs-button` → `song_catalog_page`\n  - `my-playlists-button` → `playlists_page`\n  - `trending-artists-button` → `artists_page`\n\n---\n\n### Template: song_catalog.html\n- Template File Path: templates/song_catalog.html\n- Page Title: \"Song Catalog\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Song Catalog\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Song Catalog\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `catalog-page` (Div)\n  - `search-input` (Input)\n  - `genre-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `songs-grid` (Div)\n  - `add-to-playlist-button-{{ song.song_id }}` (Button) — dynamic, one per song card\n- Context Variables:\n  - `songs`: List of dicts, each with keys: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `album_name`(str), `genre`(str), `duration`(int)\n  - `genres`: List of strings representing genre names for filter dropdown\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Button IDs follow pattern `add-to-playlist-button-<song_id>` → likely calls an action route to add that song\n\n---\n\n### Template: song_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/song_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Song Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Song Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `song.title` rendered in element with id `song-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `song-details-page` (Div)\n  - `song-title` (H1)\n  - `artist-name` (Div) — includes a link to artist profile\n  - `album-name` (Div)\n  - `duration-display` (Div)\n  - `play-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `song`: Dict with fields: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_id`(int), `artist_name`(str), `album_id`(int), `album_name`(str), `duration`(int), `genre`(str), `release_date`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `artist-name` link → `artist_profile_page` with `artist_id`\n  - `play-button` triggers play action (likely JS, no route)\n\n---\n\n### Template: playlists.html\n- Template File Path: templates/playlists.html\n- Page Title: \"My Playlists\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"My Playlists\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"My Playlists\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `playlists-page` (Div)\n  - `playlists-grid` (Div)\n  - `create-playlist-button` (Button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n  - `view-playlist-button-{{ playlist.playlist_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per playlist\n- Context Variables:\n  - `playlists`: List of dicts with keys: `playlist_id`(int), `title`(str), `description`(str), `creation_date`(str), `total_songs`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `create-playlist-button` → `create_playlist_page`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `dashboard_page`\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-playlist-button-<playlist_id>` → `playlist_details_page` with `playlist_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: playlist_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/playlist_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Playlist Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Playlist Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `playlist.title` rendered in element with id `playlist-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `playlist-details-page` (Div)\n  - `playlist-title` (H1)\n  - `playlist-description` (Div)\n  - `songs-in-playlist` (Table)\n  - `remove-song-button-{{ song.song_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per song in playlist\n  - `delete-playlist-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `playlist`: Dict with fields `playlist_id`(int), `title`(str), `description`(str), `creation_date`(str), `total_songs`(int)\n  - `songs_in_playlist`: List of dicts, each with keys `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `duration`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `delete-playlist-button` triggers route to delete playlist\n  - Buttons with pattern `remove-song-button-<song_id>` trigger remove that song from playlist\n\n---\n\n### Template: create_playlist.html\n- Template File Path: templates/create_playlist.html\n- Page Title: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `create-playlist-page` (Div)\n  - `playlist-name-input` (Input)\n  - `playlist-description-input` (Textarea)\n  - `save-playlist-button` (Button)\n  - `cancel-create-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables: None (page for creating, no dynamic data needed)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `cancel-create-button` → return to `playlists_page`\n\n---\n\n### Template: albums.html\n- Template File Path: templates/albums.html\n- Page Title: \"Albums\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Albums\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Albums\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `albums-page` (Div)\n  - `albums-grid` (Div)\n  - `search-albums` (Input)\n  - `sort-albums` (Dropdown)\n  - `view-album-button-{{ album.album_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per album\n- Context Variables:\n  - `albums`: List of dicts with keys: `album_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `release_year`(int), `genre`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-album-button-<album_id>` → `album_details_page` with `album_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: album_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/album_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Album Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Album Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `album.title` in element with id `album-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `album-details-page` (Div)\n  - `album-title` (H1)\n  - `album-artist` (Div)\n  - `album-year` (Div)\n  - `album-songs-list` (Div)\n  - `add-album-to-playlist-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `album`: Dict with fields `album_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_id`(int), `artist_name`(str), `release_year`(int), `total_songs`(int), `genre`(str)\n  - `songs_in_album`: List of dicts with keys `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `duration`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-album-to-playlist-button` triggers POST to add all album songs to a playlist\n\n---\n\n### Template: artists.html\n- Template File Path: templates/artists.html\n- Page Title: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `artists-page` (Div)\n  - `artists-grid` (Div)\n  - `search-artists` (Input)\n  - `artists-sort` (Dropdown)\n  - `view-artist-button-{{ artist.artist_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per artist\n- Context Variables:\n  - `artists`: List of dicts with keys: `artist_id`(int), `name`(str), `genre`(str), `country`(str), `formation_year`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-artist-button-<artist_id>` → `artist_profile_page` with `artist_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: genres.html\n- Template File Path: templates/genres.html\n- Page Title: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `genres-page` (Div)\n  - `genres-list` (Div)\n  - `select-genre` (Dropdown)\n  - `genre-songs` (Div)\n  - `genre-artists` (Div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `genres`: List of dicts with keys: `genre_id`(int), `genre_name`(str), `description`(str)\n  - `selected_genre`: str (optional)\n  - `selected_genre_songs`: List of dicts {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} (optional)\n  - `selected_genre_artists`: List of dicts {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} (optional)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `dashboard_page`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n---\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/songs.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `song_id` (int): Unique song identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Title of the song\n  3. `artist_id` (int): Reference to artist (foreign key from artists.txt)\n  4. `album_id` (int): Reference to album (foreign key from albums.txt)\n  5. `genre` (str): Genre name\n  6. `duration` (int): Duration of song in seconds\n  7. `release_date` (str): Release date in YYYY-MM-DD\n  8. `play_count` (int): Number of times song has been played\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/artists.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `artist_id` (int): Unique artist identifier\n  2. `name` (str): Artist name\n  3. `genre` (str): Primary genre\n  4. `country` (str): Country of origin\n  5. `formation_year` (int): Year artist/group was formed\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/albums.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `album_id` (int): Unique album identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Album title\n  3. `artist_id` (int): Reference to artist (foreign key from artists.txt)\n  4. `release_year` (int): Year album was released\n  5. `total_songs` (int): Number of songs in album\n  6. `genre` (str): Genre of album\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/genres.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `genre_id` (int): Unique genre identifier\n  2. `genre_name` (str): Genre name\n  3. `description` (str): Short description\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/playlists.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `playlist_id` (int): Unique playlist identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Playlist title\n  3. `description` (str): Playlist description\n  4. `creation_date` (str): Creation date in YYYY-MM-DD\n  5. `total_songs` (int): Number of songs in playlist\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/playlist_songs.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `playlist_song_id` (int): Unique identifier for entry\n  2. `playlist_id` (int): Reference to playlist (foreign key from playlists.txt)\n  3. `song_id` (int): Reference to song (foreign key from songs.txt)\n  4. `added_date` (str): Date song was added in YYYY-MM-DD\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|1|2|2025-01-15\n2|1|3|2025-01-15\n3|2|1|2025-01-16\n```\n\n---\n\n# End of design_spec.md\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'MusicStreaming' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'MusicStreaming' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search for songs, create and manage playlists, browse albums, explore artist profiles, filter by genres, and view song/artist statistics. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'MusicStreaming' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' web application will consist of the following ten pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Music Streaming Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured songs, trending artists, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-songs** - Type: Div - Display of featured song recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-songs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to song catalog page.\n  - **ID: my-playlists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my playlists page.\n  - **ID: trending-artists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending artists page.\n\n### 2. Song Catalog Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Catalog\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available songs with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search songs by title, artist, or album.\n  - **ID: genre-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by genre (Pop, Rock, Hip-Hop, Jazz, Classical, etc.).\n  - **ID: songs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying song cards with cover art, title, artist, and duration.\n  - **ID: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add song to playlist (each song card has this).\n\n### 3. Song Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific song.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: song-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the song details page.\n  - **ID: song-title** - Type: H1 - Display song title.\n  - **ID: artist-name** - Type: Div - Display artist name with link to artist profile.\n  - **ID: album-name** - Type: Div - Display album name.\n  - **ID: duration-display** - Type: Div - Display song duration.\n  - **ID: play-button** - Type: Button - Button to play the song.\n\n### 4. Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: My Playlists\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all user-created playlists.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlists page.\n  - **ID: playlists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying playlist cards with cover, title, and song count.\n  - **ID: create-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to create a new playlist.\n  - **ID: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view playlist details (each playlist has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. Playlist Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Playlist Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying songs in a specific playlist with management options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlist-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlist details page.\n  - **ID: playlist-title** - Type: H1 - Display playlist title.\n  - **ID: playlist-description** - Type: Div - Display playlist description.\n  - **ID: songs-in-playlist** - Type: Table - Table displaying songs with title, artist, duration, and remove option.\n  - **ID: remove-song-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove song from playlist (each song has this).\n  - **ID: delete-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to delete the entire playlist.\n\n### 6. Create Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Create New Playlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to create a new playlist with title and description.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: create-playlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the create playlist page.\n  - **ID: playlist-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input playlist name.\n  - **ID: playlist-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input playlist description.\n  - **ID: save-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to save and create the new playlist.\n  - **ID: cancel-create-button** - Type: Button - Button to cancel and go back.\n\n### 7. Album Browse Page\n- **Page Title**: Albums\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available albums with browsing and filtering options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: albums-page** - Type: Div - Container for the albums page.\n  - **ID: albums-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying album cards with cover art, title, artist, and year.\n  - **ID: search-albums** - Type: Input - Field to search albums by title or artist.\n  - **ID: sort-albums** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort albums (By Title, By Artist, By Year).\n  - **ID: view-album-button-{album_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view album details (each album has this).\n\n### 8. Album Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Album Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all songs in a specific album.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: album-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the album details page.\n  - **ID: album-title** - Type: H1 - Display album title.\n  - **ID: album-artist** - Type: Div - Display album artist.\n  - **ID: album-year** - Type: Div - Display album release year.\n  - **ID: album-songs-list** - Type: Div - List of songs in the album.\n  - **ID: add-album-to-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to add all songs from album to playlist.\n\n### 9. Artist Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: Artist Profiles\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all artists and their information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: artists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the artists page.\n  - **ID: artists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying artist cards with photo, name, and genre.\n  - **ID: search-artists** - Type: Input - Field to search artists by name.\n  - **ID: artists-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort artists (By Name, By Genre).\n  - **ID: view-artist-button-{artist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view artist profile (each artist has this).\n\n### 10. Genre Exploration Page\n- **Page Title**: Genre Exploration\n- **Overview**: A page for exploring music by genres with featured songs and artists per genre.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: genres-page** - Type: Div - Container for the genres page.\n  - **ID: genres-list** - Type: Div - List of all available genres.\n  - **ID: select-genre** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select and view a specific genre.\n  - **ID: genre-songs** - Type: Div - Display songs for selected genre.\n  - **ID: genre-artists** - Type: Div - Display artists for selected genre.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  song_id|title|artist_id|album_id|genre|duration|release_date|play_count\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n  2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n  3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n  ```\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- **File Name**: `artists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  artist_id|name|genre|country|formation_year\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n  2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n  3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n  ```\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- **File Name**: `albums.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  album_id|title|artist_id|release_year|total_songs|genre\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n  2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n  3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n  ```\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- **File Name**: `genres.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  genre_id|genre_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n  2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n  3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n  ```\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- **File Name**: `playlists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_id|title|description|creation_date|total_songs\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n  2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n  3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n  ```\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `playlist_songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_song_id|playlist_id|song_id|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|1|3|2025-01-15\n  3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n",

Backend Developer)\n\n| Route Path               | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File             | Context Variables                                                                                                    |\n|--------------------------|-------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| /                        | root_redirect           | GET            | -                         | - Redirects to `/dashboard`                                                                                         |\n| /dashboard               | dashboard_page          | GET            | dashboard.html            | featured_songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, album_name: str, duration: int}\ntrending_artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} |\n| /songs                   | song_catalog_page       | GET            | song_catalog.html         | songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, album_name: str, genre: str, duration: int}\ngenres: list of str (genre names for dropdown) |\n| /songs/search            | song_catalog_search     | POST           | song_catalog.html         | songs: filtered list (same structure as `/songs` GET)\ngenres: list of str | \n| /songs/<int:song_id>     | song_details_page       | GET            | song_details.html         | song: dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_id: int, artist_name: str, album_id: int, album_name: str, duration: int, genre: str, release_date: str}\n |\n| /playlists               | playlists_page          | GET            | playlists.html            | playlists: list of dict {playlist_id: int, title: str, description: str, creation_date: str, total_songs: int}         |\n| /playlists/create        | create_playlist_page    | GET            | create_playlist.html      | -                                                                                                                   |\n| /playlists/create        | create_playlist_submit  | POST           | - (redirect after creation)| Form fields: title (str), description (str)                                                                           |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id> | playlist_details_page  | GET            | playlist_details.html      | playlist: dict {playlist_id: int, title: str, description: str, creation_date: str, total_songs: int}\nsongs_in_playlist: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id>/delete | delete_playlist | POST           | - (redirect after deletion) | playlist_id: int                                                                                                |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id>/remove_song/<int:song_id> | remove_song_from_playlist | POST | - (redirect after removal) | playlist_id: int, song_id: int                                                                                       |\n| /albums                  | albums_page             | GET            | albums.html               | albums: list of dict {album_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, release_year: int, genre: str}                     |\n| /albums/search           | albums_search           | POST           | albums.html               | albums: filtered list (same structure as `/albums` GET)                                                             |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>   | album_details_page      | GET            | album_details.html        | album: dict {album_id: int, title: str, artist_id: int, artist_name: str, release_year: int, total_songs: int, genre: str}\nsongs_in_album: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, duration: int} |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>/add_all_to_playlist | add_album_to_playlist | POST | - (redirect after action) | album_id: int, playlist_id: int                                                                                      |\n| /artists                 | artists_page            | GET            | artists.html              | artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str, country: str, formation_year: int}                       |\n| /artists/search          | artists_search          | POST           | artists.html              | artists: filtered list (same structure as `/artists` GET)                                                           |\n| /artists/<int:artist_id> | artist_profile_page     | GET            | artist_profile.html       | artist: dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str, country: str, formation_year: int}\nsongs_by_artist: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, album_name: str, duration: int} |\n| /genres                  | genre_exploration_page  | GET            | genres.html               | genres: list of dict {genre_id: int, genre_name: str, description: str}\nselected_genre_songs: list of dict {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} (optional)\nselected_genre_artists: list of dict {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} (optional)\nselected_genre: str (genre name, optional) |\n| /genres/select           | genre_select            | POST           | genres.html               | Same as GET `/genres` plus selected_genre: str                                                                        |\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)\n\n---\n\n### Template: dashboard.html\n- Template File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Music Streaming Dashboard\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div)\n  - `featured-songs` (Div)\n  - `browse-songs-button` (Button)\n  - `my-playlists-button` (Button)\n  - `trending-artists-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `featured_songs`: List of dicts with keys: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `album_name`(str), `duration`(int seconds)\n  - `trending_artists`: List of dicts with keys: `artist_id`(int), `name`(str), `genre`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `browse-songs-button` → `song_catalog_page`\n  - `my-playlists-button` → `playlists_page`\n  - `trending-artists-button` → `artists_page`\n\n---\n\n### Template: song_catalog.html\n- Template File Path: templates/song_catalog.html\n- Page Title: \"Song Catalog\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Song Catalog\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Song Catalog\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `catalog-page` (Div)\n  - `search-input` (Input)\n  - `genre-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `songs-grid` (Div)\n  - `add-to-playlist-button-{{ song.song_id }}` (Button) — dynamic, one per song card\n- Context Variables:\n  - `songs`: List of dicts, each with keys: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `album_name`(str), `genre`(str), `duration`(int)\n  - `genres`: List of strings representing genre names for filter dropdown\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Button IDs follow pattern `add-to-playlist-button-<song_id>` → likely calls an action route to add that song\n\n---\n\n### Template: song_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/song_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Song Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Song Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `song.title` rendered in element with id `song-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `song-details-page` (Div)\n  - `song-title` (H1)\n  - `artist-name` (Div) — includes a link to artist profile\n  - `album-name` (Div)\n  - `duration-display` (Div)\n  - `play-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `song`: Dict with fields: `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_id`(int), `artist_name`(str), `album_id`(int), `album_name`(str), `duration`(int), `genre`(str), `release_date`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `artist-name` link → `artist_profile_page` with `artist_id`\n  - `play-button` triggers play action (likely JS, no route)\n\n---\n\n### Template: playlists.html\n- Template File Path: templates/playlists.html\n- Page Title: \"My Playlists\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"My Playlists\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"My Playlists\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `playlists-page` (Div)\n  - `playlists-grid` (Div)\n  - `create-playlist-button` (Button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n  - `view-playlist-button-{{ playlist.playlist_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per playlist\n- Context Variables:\n  - `playlists`: List of dicts with keys: `playlist_id`(int), `title`(str), `description`(str), `creation_date`(str), `total_songs`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `create-playlist-button` → `create_playlist_page`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `dashboard_page`\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-playlist-button-<playlist_id>` → `playlist_details_page` with `playlist_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: playlist_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/playlist_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Playlist Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Playlist Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `playlist.title` rendered in element with id `playlist-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `playlist-details-page` (Div)\n  - `playlist-title` (H1)\n  - `playlist-description` (Div)\n  - `songs-in-playlist` (Table)\n  - `remove-song-button-{{ song.song_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per song in playlist\n  - `delete-playlist-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `playlist`: Dict with fields `playlist_id`(int), `title`(str), `description`(str), `creation_date`(str), `total_songs`(int)\n  - `songs_in_playlist`: List of dicts, each with keys `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `duration`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `delete-playlist-button` triggers route to delete playlist\n  - Buttons with pattern `remove-song-button-<song_id>` trigger remove that song from playlist\n\n---\n\n### Template: create_playlist.html\n- Template File Path: templates/create_playlist.html\n- Page Title: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Create New Playlist\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `create-playlist-page` (Div)\n  - `playlist-name-input` (Input)\n  - `playlist-description-input` (Textarea)\n  - `save-playlist-button` (Button)\n  - `cancel-create-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables: None (page for creating, no dynamic data needed)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `cancel-create-button` → return to `playlists_page`\n\n---\n\n### Template: albums.html\n- Template File Path: templates/albums.html\n- Page Title: \"Albums\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Albums\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Albums\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `albums-page` (Div)\n  - `albums-grid` (Div)\n  - `search-albums` (Input)\n  - `sort-albums` (Dropdown)\n  - `view-album-button-{{ album.album_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per album\n- Context Variables:\n  - `albums`: List of dicts with keys: `album_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_name`(str), `release_year`(int), `genre`(str)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-album-button-<album_id>` → `album_details_page` with `album_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: album_details.html\n- Template File Path: templates/album_details.html\n- Page Title: \"Album Details\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Album Details\"\n- `<h1>` Content: (dynamic) `album.title` in element with id `album-title`\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `album-details-page` (Div)\n  - `album-title` (H1)\n  - `album-artist` (Div)\n  - `album-year` (Div)\n  - `album-songs-list` (Div)\n  - `add-album-to-playlist-button` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `album`: Dict with fields `album_id`(int), `title`(str), `artist_id`(int), `artist_name`(str), `release_year`(int), `total_songs`(int), `genre`(str)\n  - `songs_in_album`: List of dicts with keys `song_id`(int), `title`(str), `duration`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-album-to-playlist-button` triggers POST to add all album songs to a playlist\n\n---\n\n### Template: artists.html\n- Template File Path: templates/artists.html\n- Page Title: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Artist Profiles\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `artists-page` (Div)\n  - `artists-grid` (Div)\n  - `search-artists` (Input)\n  - `artists-sort` (Dropdown)\n  - `view-artist-button-{{ artist.artist_id }}` (Button) — dynamic per artist\n- Context Variables:\n  - `artists`: List of dicts with keys: `artist_id`(int), `name`(str), `genre`(str), `country`(str), `formation_year`(int)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Buttons with pattern `view-artist-button-<artist_id>` → `artist_profile_page` with `artist_id`\n\n---\n\n### Template: genres.html\n- Template File Path: templates/genres.html\n- Page Title: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- `<title>` Content: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- `<h1>` Content: \"Genre Exploration\"\n- Required Element IDs and Types:\n  - `genres-page` (Div)\n  - `genres-list` (Div)\n  - `select-genre` (Dropdown)\n  - `genre-songs` (Div)\n  - `genre-artists` (Div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `genres`: List of dicts with keys: `genre_id`(int), `genre_name`(str), `description`(str)\n  - `selected_genre`: str (optional)\n  - `selected_genre_songs`: List of dicts {song_id: int, title: str, artist_name: str, duration: int} (optional)\n  - `selected_genre_artists`: List of dicts {artist_id: int, name: str, genre: str} (optional)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `dashboard_page`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n---\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/songs.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `song_id` (int): Unique song identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Title of the song\n  3. `artist_id` (int): Reference to artist (foreign key from artists.txt)\n  4. `album_id` (int): Reference to album (foreign key from albums.txt)\n  5. `genre` (str): Genre name\n  6. `duration` (int): Duration of song in seconds\n  7. `release_date` (str): Release date in YYYY-MM-DD\n  8. `play_count` (int): Number of times song has been played\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/artists.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `artist_id` (int): Unique artist identifier\n  2. `name` (str): Artist name\n  3. `genre` (str): Primary genre\n  4. `country` (str): Country of origin\n  5. `formation_year` (int): Year artist/group was formed\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/albums.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `album_id` (int): Unique album identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Album title\n  3. `artist_id` (int): Reference to artist (foreign key from artists.txt)\n  4. `release_year` (int): Year album was released\n  5. `total_songs` (int): Number of songs in album\n  6. `genre` (str): Genre of album\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/genres.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `genre_id` (int): Unique genre identifier\n  2. `genre_name` (str): Genre name\n  3. `description` (str): Short description\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/playlists.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `playlist_id` (int): Unique playlist identifier\n  2. `title` (str): Playlist title\n  3. `description` (str): Playlist description\n  4. `creation_date` (str): Creation date in YYYY-MM-DD\n  5. `total_songs` (int): Number of songs in playlist\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- Filename and Path: `data/playlist_songs.txt`\n- File Format: Pipe-delimited `|`\n- Fields (in order):\n  1. `playlist_song_id` (int): Unique identifier for entry\n  2. `playlist_id` (int): Reference to playlist (foreign key from playlists.txt)\n  3. `song_id` (int): Reference to song (foreign key from songs.txt)\n  4. `added_date` (str): Date song was added in YYYY-MM-DD\n- Example Rows:\n```\n1|1|2|2025-01-15\n2|1|3|2025-01-15\n3|2|1|2025-01-16\n```\n\n---\n\n# End of design_spec.md\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'MusicStreaming' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'MusicStreaming' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search for songs, create and manage playlists, browse albums, explore artist profiles, filter by genres, and view song/artist statistics. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'MusicStreaming' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' web application will consist of the following ten pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Music Streaming Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured songs, trending artists, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-songs** - Type: Div - Display of featured song recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-songs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to song catalog page.\n  - **ID: my-playlists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my playlists page.\n  - **ID: trending-artists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending artists page.\n\n### 2. Song Catalog Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Catalog\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available songs with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search songs by title, artist, or album.\n  - **ID: genre-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by genre (Pop, Rock, Hip-Hop, Jazz, Classical, etc.).\n  - **ID: songs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying song cards with cover art, title, artist, and duration.\n  - **ID: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add song to playlist (each song card has this).\n\n### 3. Song Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific song.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: song-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the song details page.\n  - **ID: song-title** - Type: H1 - Display song title.\n  - **ID: artist-name** - Type: Div - Display artist name with link to artist profile.\n  - **ID: album-name** - Type: Div - Display album name.\n  - **ID: duration-display** - Type: Div - Display song duration.\n  - **ID: play-button** - Type: Button - Button to play the song.\n\n### 4. Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: My Playlists\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all user-created playlists.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlists page.\n  - **ID: playlists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying playlist cards with cover, title, and song count.\n  - **ID: create-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to create a new playlist.\n  - **ID: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view playlist details (each playlist has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. Playlist Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Playlist Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying songs in a specific playlist with management options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlist-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlist details page.\n  - **ID: playlist-title** - Type: H1 - Display playlist title.\n  - **ID: playlist-description** - Type: Div - Display playlist description.\n  - **ID: songs-in-playlist** - Type: Table - Table displaying songs with title, artist, duration, and remove option.\n  - **ID: remove-song-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove song from playlist (each song has this).\n  - **ID: delete-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to delete the entire playlist.\n\n### 6. Create Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Create New Playlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to create a new playlist with title and description.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: create-playlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the create playlist page.\n  - **ID: playlist-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input playlist name.\n  - **ID: playlist-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input playlist description.\n  - **ID: save-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to save and create the new playlist.\n  - **ID: cancel-create-button** - Type: Button - Button to cancel and go back.\n\n### 7. Album Browse Page\n- **Page Title**: Albums\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available albums with browsing and filtering options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: albums-page** - Type: Div - Container for the albums page.\n  - **ID: albums-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying album cards with cover art, title, artist, and year.\n  - **ID: search-albums** - Type: Input - Field to search albums by title or artist.\n  - **ID: sort-albums** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort albums (By Title, By Artist, By Year).\n  - **ID: view-album-button-{album_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view album details (each album has this).\n\n### 8. Album Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Album Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all songs in a specific album.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: album-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the album details page.\n  - **ID: album-title** - Type: H1 - Display album title.\n  - **ID: album-artist** - Type: Div - Display album artist.\n  - **ID: album-year** - Type: Div - Display album release year.\n  - **ID: album-songs-list** - Type: Div - List of songs in the album.\n  - **ID: add-album-to-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to add all songs from album to playlist.\n\n### 9. Artist Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: Artist Profiles\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all artists and their information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: artists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the artists page.\n  - **ID: artists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying artist cards with photo, name, and genre.\n  - **ID: search-artists** - Type: Input - Field to search artists by name.\n  - **ID: artists-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort artists (By Name, By Genre).\n  - **ID: view-artist-button-{artist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view artist profile (each artist has this).\n\n### 10. Genre Exploration Page\n- **Page Title**: Genre Exploration\n- **Overview**: A page for exploring music by genres with featured songs and artists per genre.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: genres-page** - Type: Div - Container for the genres page.\n  - **ID: genres-list** - Type: Div - List of all available genres.\n  - **ID: select-genre** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select and view a specific genre.\n  - **ID: genre-songs** - Type: Div - Display songs for selected genre.\n  - **ID: genre-artists** - Type: Div - Display artists for selected genre.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  song_id|title|artist_id|album_id|genre|duration|release_date|play_count\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n  2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n  3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n  ```\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- **File Name**: `artists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  artist_id|name|genre|country|formation_year\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n  2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n  3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n  ```\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- **File Name**: `albums.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  album_id|title|artist_id|release_year|total_songs|genre\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n  2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n  3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n  ```\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- **File Name**: `genres.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  genre_id|genre_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n  2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n  3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n  ```\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- **File Name**: `playlists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_id|title|description|creation_date|total_songs\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n  2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n  3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n  ```\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `playlist_songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_song_id|playlist_id|song_id|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|1|3|2025-01-15\n  3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n",

         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         
         # Data file paths
         SONGS_FILE = 'data/songs.txt'
         ARTISTS_FILE = 'data/artists.txt'
         ALBUMS_FILE = 'data/albums.txt'
         GENRES_FILE = 'data/genres.txt'
         PLAYLISTS_FILE = 'data/playlists.txt'
         PLAYLIST_SONGS_FILE = 'data/playlist_songs.txt'
         
         # Helper functions to read data from files
         
         def read_songs():
             songs = []
             if not os.path.exists(SONGS_FILE):
                 return songs
             with open(SONGS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 8:
                         continue
                     try:
                         song_id = int(parts[0])
                         title = parts[1]
                         artist_id = int(parts[2])
                         album_id = int(parts[3])
                         genre = parts[4]
                         duration = int(parts[5])
                         release_date = parts[6]
                         play_count = int(parts[7])
                         songs.append({
                             'song_id': song_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'artist_id': artist_id,
                             'album_id': album_id,
                             'genre': genre,
                             'duration': duration,
                             'release_date': release_date,
                             'play_count': play_count
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return songs
         
         def read_artists():
             artists = []
             if not os.path.exists(ARTISTS_FILE):
                 return artists
             with open(ARTISTS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 5:
                         continue
                     try:
                         artist_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         genre = parts[2]
                         country = parts[3]
                         formation_year = int(parts[4])
                         artists.append({
                             'artist_id': artist_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'genre': genre,
                             'country': country,
                             'formation_year': formation_year
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return artists
         
         def read_albums():
             albums = []
             if not os.path.exists(ALBUMS_FILE):
                 return albums
             with open(ALBUMS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         album_id = int(parts[0])
                         title = parts[1]
                         artist_id = int(parts[2])
                         release_year = int(parts[3])
                         total_songs = int(parts[4])
                         genre = parts[5]
                         albums.append({
                             'album_id': album_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'artist_id': artist_id,
                             'release_year': release_year,
                             'total_songs': total_songs,
                             'genre': genre
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return albums
         
         def read_genres():
             genres = []
             if not os.path.exists(GENRES_FILE):
                 return genres
             with open(GENRES_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 3:
                         continue
                     try:
                         genre_id = int(parts[0])
                         genre_name = parts[1]
                         description = parts[2]
                         genres.append({
                             'genre_id': genre_id,
                             'genre_name': genre_name,
                             'description': description
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return genres
         
         def read_playlists():
             playlists = []
             if not os.path.exists(PLAYLISTS_FILE):
                 return playlists
             with open(PLAYLISTS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 5:
                         continue
                     try:
                         playlist_id = int(parts[0])
                         title = parts[1]
                         description = parts[2]
                         creation_date = parts[3]
                         total_songs = int(parts[4])
                         playlists.append({
                             'playlist_id': playlist_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'description': description,
                             'creation_date': creation_date,
                             'total_songs': total_songs
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return playlists
         
         def read_playlist_songs():
             playlist_songs = []
             if not os.path.exists(PLAYLIST_SONGS_FILE):
                 return playlist_songs
             with open(PLAYLIST_SONGS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 4:
                         continue
                     try:
                         playlist_song_id = int(parts[0])
                         playlist_id = int(parts[1])
                         song_id = int(parts[2])
                         added_date = parts[3]
                         playlist_songs.append({
                             'playlist_song_id': playlist_song_id,
                             'playlist_id': playlist_id,
                             'song_id': song_id,
                             'added_date': added_date
                         })
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return playlist_songs
         
         # Helper functions to write data
         
         def write_playlists(playlists):
             with open(PLAYLISTS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for p in playlists:
                     row = f"{p['playlist_id']}|{p['title']}|{p['description']}|{p['creation_date']}|{p['total_songs']}"
                     f.write(row + '\n')
         
         
         def write_playlist_songs(playlist_songs):
             with open(PLAYLIST_SONGS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for ps in playlist_songs:
                     row = f"{ps['playlist_song_id']}|{ps['playlist_id']}|{ps['song_id']}|{ps['added_date']}"
                     f.write(row + '\n')
         
         # Helper to generate next ids
         
         def get_next_playlist_id(playlists):
             if not playlists:
                 return 1
             return max(p['playlist_id'] for p in playlists) + 1
         
         def get_next_playlist_song_id(playlist_songs):
             if not playlist_songs:
                 return 1
             return max(ps['playlist_song_id'] for ps in playlist_songs) + 1
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def get_artist_by_id(artist_id):
             artists = read_artists()
             for a in artists:
                 if a['artist_id'] == artist_id:
                     return a
             return None
         
         def get_album_by_id(album_id):
             albums = read_albums()
             for a in albums:
                 if a['album_id'] == album_id:
                     return a
             return None
         
         def get_song_by_id(song_id):
             songs = read_songs()
             for s in songs:
                 if s['song_id'] == song_id:
                     return s
             return None
         
         # Route implementations
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard_page():
             songs = read_songs()
             artists = read_artists()
             albums = read_albums()
         
             # Featured songs: We pick top 5 played songs sorted by play_count descending
             top_songs = sorted(songs, key=lambda s: s['play_count'], reverse=True)[:5]
             featured_songs = []
             for s in top_songs:
                 artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
                 album = get_album_by_id(s['album_id'])
                 if artist is None or album is None:
                     continue
                 featured_songs.append({
                     'song_id': s['song_id'],
                     'title': s['title'],
                     'artist_name': artist['name'],
                     'album_name': album['title'],
                     'duration': s['duration']
                 })
         
             # Trending artists: top 5 artists with highest total play counts on their songs
             artist_play_counts = {}
             for s in songs:
                 if s['artist_id'] in artist_play_counts:
                     artist_play_counts[s['artist_id']] += s['play_count']
                 else:
                     artist_play_counts[s['artist_id']] = s['play_count']
         
             trending_artists_ids = sorted(artist_play_counts, key=lambda aid: artist_play_counts[aid], reverse=True)[:5]
             trending_artists = []
             for aid in trending_artists_ids:
                 artist = get_artist_by_id(aid)
                 if artist is None:
                     continue
                 trending_artists.append({
                     'artist_id': artist['artist_id'],
                     'name': artist['name'],
                     'genre': artist['genre']
                 })
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_songs=featured_songs, trending_artists=trending_artists)
         
         @app.route('/songs', methods=['GET'])
         def song_catalog_page():
             songs = read_songs()
             artists = read_artists()
             albums = read_albums()
             genres = sorted(set(s['genre'] for s in songs))
         
             # Build songs list with artist_name and album_name
             songs_list = []
             for s in songs:
                 artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
                 album = get_album_by_id(s['album_id'])
                 if artist is None or album is None:
                     continue
                 songs_list.append({
                     'song_id': s['song_id'],
                     'title': s['title'],
                     'artist_name': artist['name'],
                     'album_name': album['title'],
                     'genre': s['genre'],
                     'duration': s['duration']
                 })
         
             return render_template('song_catalog.html', songs=songs_list, genres=genres)
         
         @app.route('/songs/search', methods=['POST'])
         def song_catalog_search():
             search_text = request.form.get('search_input', '').strip().lower()
             selected_genre = request.form.get('genre_filter', '')
         
             songs = read_songs()
             artists = read_artists()
             albums = read_albums()
         
             def song_matches(s):
                 match_text = (s['title'].lower())
                 if search_text and search_text not in match_text:
                     return False
                 if selected_genre and selected_genre != "All Genres" and s['genre'] != selected_genre:
                     return False
                 return True
         
             filtered = []
             for s in songs:
                 if not song_matches(s):
                     continue
                 artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
                 album = get_album_by_id(s['album_id'])
                 if artist is None or album is None:
                     continue
                 filtered.append({
                     'song_id': s['song_id'],
                     'title': s['title'],
                     'artist_name': artist['name'],
                     'album_name': album['title'],
                     'genre': s['genre'],
                     'duration': s['duration']
                 })
         
             genres = sorted(set(s['genre'] for s in songs))
         
             return render_template('song_catalog.html', songs=filtered, genres=genres)
         
         @app.route('/songs/<int:song_id>')
         def song_details_page(song_id):
             s = get_song_by_id(song_id)
             if s is None:
                 abort(404)
             artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
             album = get_album_by_id(s['album_id'])
             if artist is None or album is None:
                 abort(404)
             song = {
                 'song_id': s['song_id'],
                 'title': s['title'],
                 'artist_id': artist['artist_id'],
                 'artist_name': artist['name'],
                 'album_id': album['album_id'],
                 'album_name': album['title'],
                 'duration': s['duration'],
                 'genre': s['genre'],
                 'release_date': s['release_date']
             }
             return render_template('song_details.html', song=song)
         
         @app.route('/playlists')
         def playlists_page():
             playlists = read_playlists()
             return render_template('playlists.html', playlists=playlists)
         
         @app.route('/playlists/create', methods=['GET'])
         def create_playlist_page():
             return render_template('create_playlist.html')
         
         @app.route('/playlists/create', methods=['POST'])
         def create_playlist_submit():
             title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
             description = request.form.get('description', '').strip()
         
             if not title:
                 # Simple validation: Require title
                 return redirect(url_for('create_playlist_page'))
         
             playlists = read_playlists()
             playlist_songs = read_playlist_songs()
         
             new_id = get_next_playlist_id(playlists)
             creation_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             new_playlist = {
                 'playlist_id': new_id,
                 'title': title,
                 'description': description,
                 'creation_date': creation_date,
                 'total_songs': 0
             }
             playlists.append(new_playlist)
             write_playlists(playlists)
         
             # Redirect to playlist details page of the newly created playlist
             return redirect(url_for('playlist_details_page', playlist_id=new_id))
         
         @app.route('/playlists/<int:playlist_id>')
         def playlist_details_page(playlist_id):
             playlists = read_playlists()
             playlist = next((p for p in playlists if p['playlist_id'] == playlist_id), None)
             if playlist is None:
                 abort(404)
         
             playlist_songs = read_playlist_songs()
             songs = read_songs()
             artists = read_artists()
         
             # Get songs in playlist
             songs_in_playlist = []
             # collect song_ids in playlist
             playlist_song_ids = [ps['song_id'] for ps in playlist_songs if ps['playlist_id'] == playlist_id]
         
             for song_id in playlist_song_ids:
                 s = next((song for song in songs if song['song_id'] == song_id), None)
                 if s is None:
                     continue
                 artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
                 if artist is None:
                     continue
                 songs_in_playlist.append({
                     'song_id': s['song_id'],
                     'title': s['title'],
                     'artist_name': artist['name'],
                     'duration': s['duration']
                 })
         
             return render_template('playlist_details.html', playlist=playlist, songs_in_playlist=songs_in_playlist)
         
         @app.route('/playlists/<int:playlist_id>/delete', methods=['POST'])
         def delete_playlist(playlist_id):
             playlists = read_playlists()
             playlist_songs = read_playlist_songs()
         
             # Remove playlist
             playlists = [p for p in playlists if p['playlist_id'] != playlist_id]
             write_playlists(playlists)
         
             # Remove all playlist songs entries for this playlist
             playlist_songs = [ps for ps in playlist_songs if ps['playlist_id'] != playlist_id]
             write_playlist_songs(playlist_songs)
         
             return redirect(url_for('playlists_page'))
         
         @app.route('/playlists/<int:playlist_id>/remove_song/<int:song_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def remove_song_from_playlist(playlist_id, song_id):
             playlist_songs = read_playlist_songs()
         
             new_playlist_songs = []
             removed = False
             for ps in playlist_songs:
                 if ps['playlist_id'] == playlist_id and ps['song_id'] == song_id and not removed:
                     removed = True
                     continue
                 new_playlist_songs.append(ps)
         
             if removed:
                 # Update playlist total songs count
                 playlists = read_playlists()
                 for p in playlists:
                     if p['playlist_id'] == playlist_id:
                         p['total_songs'] = max(0, p['total_songs'] - 1)
                         break
                 write_playlists(playlists)
                 write_playlist_songs(new_playlist_songs)
         
             return redirect(url_for('playlist_details_page', playlist_id=playlist_id))

         @app.route('/albums/<int:album_id>')
         def album_details_page(album_id):
             album = get_album_by_id(album_id)
             if album is None:
                 abort(404)
             artist = get_artist_by_id(album['artist_id'])
             if artist is None:
                 abort(404)
         
             songs = read_songs()
             songs_in_album = []
             for s in songs:
                 if s['album_id'] == album_id:
                     songs_in_album.append({
                         'song_id': s['song_id'],
                         'title': s['title'],
                         'duration': s['duration']
                     })
         
             album_dict = {
                 'album_id': album['album_id'],
                 'title': album['title'],
                 'artist_id': artist['artist_id'],
                 'artist_name': artist['name'],
                 'release_year': album['release_year'],

                 'genre': album['genre']
             }
         
             return render_template('album_details.html', album=album_dict, songs_in_album=songs_in_album)
         
         @app.route('/albums/<int:album_id>/add_all_to_playlist', methods=['POST'])
         def add_album_to_playlist(album_id):
             playlist_id = request.form.get('playlist_id', type=int)
             if playlist_id is None:
                 # Bad request
                 abort(400)
         
             album = get_album_by_id(album_id)
             if album is None:
                 abort(404)
         
             playlists = read_playlists()
             playlist = next((p for p in playlists if p['playlist_id'] == playlist_id), None)
             if playlist is None:
                 abort(404)
         
             songs = read_songs()
             playlist_songs = read_playlist_songs()
         
             # Find all songs in album
             album_songs = [s for s in songs if s['album_id'] == album_id]
         
             # Current song_ids in playlist
             current_song_ids = set(ps['song_id'] for ps in playlist_songs if ps['playlist_id'] == playlist_id)
         
             next_ps_id = get_next_playlist_song_id(playlist_songs)
             added_today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             # Add all album songs that are not yet in playlist
             for s in album_songs:
                 if s['song_id'] not in current_song_ids:
                     playlist_songs.append({
                         'playlist_song_id': next_ps_id,
                         'playlist_id': playlist_id,
                         'song_id': s['song_id'],
                         'added_date': added_today
                     })
                     next_ps_id += 1
                     playlist['total_songs'] += 1
         
             write_playlist_songs(playlist_songs)
             write_playlists(playlists)
         
             return redirect(url_for('album_details_page', album_id=album_id))

         @app.route('/genres/select', methods=['POST'])
         def genre_select():
             selected_genre = request.form.get('select_genre', '').strip()
             genres = read_genres()
         
             # Filter songs and artists by selected genre
             songs = read_songs()
             artists = read_artists()
         
             selected_songs = []
             selected_artists = []
         
             if selected_genre:
                 for s in songs:
                     if s['genre'].lower() == selected_genre.lower():
                         artist = get_artist_by_id(s['artist_id'])
                         if artist:
                             selected_songs.append({
                                 'song_id': s['song_id'],
                                 'title': s['title'],
                                 'artist_name': artist['name'],
                                 'duration': s['duration']
                             })
                 for a in artists:
                     if a['genre'].lower() == selected_genre.lower():
                         selected_artists.append({
                             'artist_id': a['artist_id'],
                             'name': a['name'],
                             'genre': a['genre']
                         })
         
             return render_template('genres.html', genres=genres, selected_genre=selected_genre,
                                    selected_genre_songs=selected_songs, selected_genre_artists=selected_artists)
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         <body>

             <h1 id="album-title">{{ album.title }}</h1>
             <div id="album-artist">Artist: {{ album.artist_name }}</div>
             <div id="album-year">Release Year: {{ album.release_year }}</div>
         
             <div id="album-songs-list">
                 <h2>Songs in Album</h2>
                 <ul>
                     {% for song in songs_in_album %}
                     <li>{{ song.title }} - {{ song.duration }} seconds</li>
                     {% endfor %}
                 </ul>
             </div>
         
             <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('add_album_to_playlist', album_id=album.album_id) }}">
                 <button type="submit" id="add-album-to-playlist-button">Add Album to Playlist</button>
             </form>
         </div>
         </body>

                     {% endfor %}
                 </select>
                 <button type="submit">Explore</button>
             </form>

             </div>

             <div id="genre-songs">
                 <h2>Songs in {{ selected_genre }}</h2>
                 <ul>
                     {% for song in selected_genre_songs %}
                     <li>{{ song.title }} by {{ song.artist_name }} - {{ song.duration }} seconds</li>
                     {% endfor %}
                 </ul>
             </div>

                     {% for artist in selected_genre_artists %}

                     {% endfor %}

             </div>
             {% endif %}
         
             <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard_page') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
         </div>
         </body>
